This message was automatically generated.



stats_part2 test appears to be flaky. Stats periodically change from complete to partial and back, with no effect on anything else. This has been going on for some time.
[~prasanth_j] do you know why this would happen? IIRC you were fixing some stats issues in explain before.

not exactly sure. But it can only change if some partitions column stats are missing. Debug logs should show what is missing. https://github.com/apache/hive/blob/master/ql/src/java/org/apache/hadoop/hive/ql/stats/StatsUtils.java#L436

The flaky test is actually for a master bug that is probably triggered by this branch somehow (still looking):
"stats.StatsUtils: Column stats requested for : 2 partitions. Able to retrieve for 3 partitions"
-Not sure why there should be more stats than requested, but this shouldn't cause stats to become partial- actually nm, maybe they should be, the number is supplied with the aggregate, and the compile side cannot just discard an extra partition. AggregateStatsCache probably has some issue, or some phantom partition is getting cached.

Disabled the aggregate stats cache for this test and filed a separate bug on master.
